Let's Logic Collection ID: 565
Title: York Shen Collection
Author: York Shen
Description: York Shen made a huge number of remodels, which are considered by many as quality and difficult. This collection has the majority of them, with duplicates already on the site removed (these duplicates are in Sasquatch remodels, Gyjgw collections, Arrangements collection and Small and medium remodels, as well as Microban remodels).
